# IIIF Field Archive Studio â€” Board Canvas Technical Specification

## Executive Summary

The Board Canvas is a dual-purpose spatial workspace that serves two distinct but interconnected workflows within the IIIF Field Archive Studio:

1. **Pre-IIIF Organization Mode**: A visual workspace for transforming unsorted field research media into Biiif-compliant folder structures
2. **Post-IIIF Annotation Mode**: A relationship mapping canvas for connecting IIIF-compliant resources using W3C Web Annotations
Make the invisible visible â€” Show clustering, relationships, and validation status spatially
Progressive disclosure â€” Simple at overview, detailed on zoom
Direct manipulation â€” Edit IIIF properties inline, not in dialogs
Continuous feedback â€” Real-time validation and preview
Guided but not constrained â€” Wizards for beginners, shortcuts for experts

Both modes share the same underlying spatial canvas infrastructure but expose different toolsets and produce different outputs. The board itself is represented as an IIIF Manifest containing a single large synthetic Canvas, with all items and connections expressed as W3C Web Annotations.
Now I have a comprehensive understanding of both the IIIF Presentation API 3.0 and the W3C Web Annotation Data Model. Let me now read the skill documentation for creating a comprehensive document.Now let me create a comprehensive technical specification document for the whiteboard/board canvas functionality that addresses both use cases: media organization for Biiif-compliant folder structures and annotation/linking between IIIF-compliant objects.I've created a comprehensive technical specification for the Board Canvas functionality in the IIIF Field Archive Studio. The document covers both use cases you mentioned:

**Dual-Mode Architecture:**
- **Organization Mode (Pre-IIIF)**: For visually organizing raw media files into Biiif-compliant folder structures through drag-and-drop, grouping, and clustering
Visual Folder Structure BuilderDrag-and-drop interface for building the Biiif hierarchy:Structure Canvas Mode

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Auto-Sequence Suggestions After drawing, the system suggests:

    "Sort by filename instead?" (if names are sequential)
    "Sort by capture time?" (if EXIF dates are sequential)
    "Reverse for right-to-left viewing?"

Extended Pattern Recognition:
Detected Pattern	Suggested Relationship
file.jpg + file.txt	Image + transcription
file.jpg + file.xml	Image + TEI/metadata
file.mp3 + file.srt	Audio + subtitles
file.mp4 + file.vtt	Video + captions
file.tif + file.jpg	Master + derivative (Choice)
file_v1.jpg + file_v2.jpg	Versions (Choice or sequence)
file.jpg + file_notes.md	Image + commentary
file.RAW + file.jpg	Raw + processed (link in metadata)

Quick Structure Actions:

    Drag files into folders
    Drag folders to nest them
    Right-click folder â†’ "Convert to Manifest" (add _ prefix)
    Right-click folder â†’ "Convert to Collection" (remove _ prefix)
    Double-click folder to expand/collapse

Interview Template pre-configures canvas sets expecting audio + transcript pairs with supplementing motivation.
Site Survey Template creates a collection structure with nested manifests for different areas, pre-tagged with navPlace expectations.
- **Annotation Mode (Post-IIIF)**: For creating scholarly connections between IIIF-compliant resources using W3C Web Annotations
Temporal Proximity: "These 5 photos were taken within 2 minutes of this audio recording - create a related group?"
Zoom Lens Mode
Hold a modifier key and hover over an item to see a magnified IIIF Image API view floating above the board. Essential for comparing fine details across items without losing spatial context.

6. Semantic Zoom with Progressive DisclosureDifferent information appears at different zoom levels:Zoom LevelVisible Information< 25%Item thumbnails only, connection lines, group boundaries25-50%+ Item labels, connection type icons50-100%+ Metadata preview, connection labels, certainty indicators100-200%+ Full metadata panels, annotation text, IIIF properties> 200%+ Deep zoom into item content, pixel-level inspectionSemantic Halos
At overview zoom, items glow with halos indicating their annotation richness:

Bright halo = many connections
Colored halo = specific connection types dominate
Pulsing halo = recent activity

âš–ï¸ = has rights
ğŸ“ = has navPlace
ğŸ“… = has navDate

â”‚  [â–¶ Play]  [Add marker]  [Link selection to board item]    â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
Drag a board item onto the timeline to create a temporal link (FragmentSelector with t= value).
**Key Technical Highlights:**

The board itself is modeled as an IIIF Manifest with a single large Canvas (10,000Ã—10,000 default), where all placed items become `painting` annotations targeting specific regions via FragmentSelectors, and all connections become `linking` annotations with multiple targets.

**IIIF/W3C Compliance Features:**
- Full W3C Web Annotation Data Model compliance with proper motivation values
- Support for all selector types (FragmentSelector, SvgSelector, etc.)
- Extended vocabulary for connection types (depicts, transcribes, contradicts, precedes/follows)
- Certainty/confidence levels for scholarly annotations
- Proper AnnotationPage layering for visibility toggling

**UX/UI Specifications:**
- Complete tool palettes for both modes
- Sidebar panel designs for sources, layers, properties, and search
- Keyboard shortcuts for efficient workflows
- Context menus and interaction patterns
- Zoom behaviors including click-to-zoom for annotations

**Technical Infrastructure:**
- Spatial indexing with R-tree for performance
- Virtualized rendering for large boards
- Thumbnail loading strategies with priority queuing
- Auto-save and project persistence formats
- Export formats for both Biiif folder structures and W3C Annotation Collections

### 1.2 Mode Switching

The board operates in two mutually exclusive modes, switchable via the mode toggle in the toolbar:

| Mode | Purpose | Item Source | Output |
|------|---------|-------------|--------|
| **Organization** | Pre-IIIF media structuring | Raw files from filesystem | Biiif folder structure |
| **Annotation** | Post-IIIF relationship mapping | IIIF Manifests/Canvases | Web Annotation Collections |

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```

---

## 2. Data Model & IIIF Compliance

### 2.1 Board as IIIF Manifest

Each board is represented as an IIIF Presentation API 3.0 Manifest containing a single synthetic Canvas:

```json
{
  "@context": "http://iiif.io/api/presentation/3/context.json",
  "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid",
  "type": "Manifest",
  "label": { "en": ["Research Board: Manuscript Analysis"] },
  "summary": { "en": ["Visual workspace for mapping relationships between manuscript fragments"] },
  "metadata": [
    {
      "label": { "en": ["Board Mode"] },
      "value": { "en": ["annotation"] }
    },
    {
      "label": { "en": ["Created"] },
      "value": { "en": ["2025-01-21T12:00:00Z"] }
    }
  ],
  "behavior": ["unordered"],
  "items": [
    {
      "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1",
      "type": "Canvas",
      "label": { "none": ["Main Board Canvas"] },
      "width": 10000,
      "height": 10000,
      "backgroundColor": "#F5F5F5",
      "items": [
        {
          "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1/page/1",
          "type": "AnnotationPage",
          "items": []
        }
      ],
      "annotations": [
        {
          "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1/annotations/1",
          "type": "AnnotationPage"
        }
      ]
    }
  ],
  "structures": []
}
```

### 2.2 Items on Board (painting Annotations)

Items placed on the board become Annotations with `motivation: "painting"`:

```json
{
  "@context": [
    "http://www.w3.org/ns/anno.jsonld",
    "http://iiif.io/api/presentation/3/context.json"
  ],
  "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/annotations/item-1",
  "type": "Annotation",
  "motivation": "painting",
  "created": "2025-01-21T12:00:00Z",
  "creator": {
    "id": "https://example.org/users/researcher-1",
    "type": "Person",
    "name": "Jane Researcher"
  },
  "body": {
    "id": "https://example.org/iiif/manifest/123/canvas/1",
    "type": "Canvas",
    "label": { "en": ["Manuscript Page 1"] },
    "thumbnail": [{
      "id": "https://example.org/iiif/image/123/full/200,/0/default.jpg",
      "type": "Image",
      "format": "image/jpeg"
    }]
  },
  "target": {
    "type": "SpecificResource",
    "source": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1",
    "selector": {
      "type": "FragmentSelector",
      "conformsTo": "http://www.w3.org/TR/media-frags/",
      "value": "xywh=100,200,400,300"
    }
  }
}
```

### 2.3 Connections (linking Annotations)

Connections between items use W3C Web Annotations with `motivation: "linking"`:

```json
{
  "@context": "http://www.w3.org/ns/anno.jsonld",
  "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/connections/conn-1",
  "type": "Annotation",
  "motivation": "linking",
  "created": "2025-01-21T12:30:00Z",
  "creator": {
    "id": "https://example.org/users/researcher-1",
    "type": "Person",
    "name": "Jane Researcher"
  },
  "body": {
    "type": "TextualBody",
    "value": "These manuscripts share the same scribal hand",
    "format": "text/plain",
    "language": "en"
  },
  "target": [
    {
      "type": "SpecificResource",
      "source": "https://example.org/iiif/manifest/123/canvas/1",
      "selector": {
        "type": "FragmentSelector",
        "conformsTo": "http://www.w3.org/TR/media-frags/",
        "value": "xywh=50,50,100,80"
      },
      "purpose": "identifying"
    },
    {
      "type": "SpecificResource",
      "source": "https://example.org/iiif/manifest/456/canvas/1",
      "selector": {
        "type": "FragmentSelector",
        "conformsTo": "http://www.w3.org/TR/media-frags/",
        "value": "xywh=200,150,120,90"
      },
      "purpose": "identifying"
    }
  ]
}
```

### 2.4 Connection Types (Extended Motivations)

The application supports semantic connection types through combined motivations and custom extensions:

```json
{
  "@context": [
    "http://www.w3.org/ns/anno.jsonld",
    {
      "fas": "https://example.org/ns/field-archive-studio#",
      "connectionType": "fas:connectionType",
      "depicts": "fas:connectionType#depicts",
      "transcribes": "fas:connectionType#transcribes",
      "contradicts": "fas:connectionType#contradicts",
      "precedes": "fas:connectionType#precedes",
      "follows": "fas:connectionType#follows",
      "relatesTo": "fas:connectionType#relatesTo",
      "partOf": "fas:connectionType#partOf",
      "sameAs": "fas:connectionType#sameAs"
    }
  ],
  "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/connections/conn-2",
  "type": "Annotation",
  "motivation": ["linking", "identifying"],
  "connectionType": "depicts",
  "body": {
    "type": "TextualBody",
    "value": "This photograph shows the exterior of the building in the architectural drawing",
    "format": "text/plain"
  },
  "target": [/* ... */]
}
```

**Connection Type Vocabulary:**

| Type | Combined Motivation | Semantic Meaning | Visual Indicator |
|------|---------------------|------------------|------------------|
| Depicts | `linking` + `identifying` | Source visually represents target | Solid line, camera icon |
| Transcribes | `linking` + `describing` | Source is textual transcription of target | Dashed line, text icon |
| Relates To | `linking` | General relationship | Thin solid line |
| Contradicts | `linking` + custom | Evidence conflicts | Red wavy line |
| Precedes | `linking` + custom | Temporal sequence (before) | Arrow, clock icon |
| Follows | `linking` + custom | Temporal sequence (after) | Arrow, clock icon |
| Part Of | `linking` + custom | Hierarchical containment | Bracket connector |
| Same As | `linking` + custom | Identity equivalence | Double-headed arrow |

### 2.5 Board Annotations (Non-Connection)

Annotations that don't connect items but add context to the board:

```json
{
  "@context": "http://www.w3.org/ns/anno.jsonld",
  "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/annotations/note-1",
  "type": "Annotation",
  "motivation": "commenting",
  "body": {
    "type": "TextualBody",
    "value": "This section needs further investigation after the archive visit",
    "format": "text/plain"
  },
  "target": {
    "type": "SpecificResource",
    "source": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1",
    "selector": {
      "type": "FragmentSelector",
      "value": "xywh=500,600,300,200"
    }
  }
}
```

**Annotation Types on Board:**

| Element | W3C Motivation | Selector Type | Body Type |
|---------|---------------|---------------|-----------|
| Sticky Note | `commenting` | FragmentSelector | TextualBody |
| Freehand Drawing | `highlighting` | SvgSelector | None (visual only) |
| Shape Highlight | `highlighting` | FragmentSelector | None or TextualBody |
| Text Label | `describing` | FragmentSelector | TextualBody |
| Frame/Section | `tagging` | FragmentSelector | TextualBody (name) |

---

## 3. Organization Mode (Pre-IIIF)

### 3.1 Purpose

Transform unsorted field research media into Biiif-compliant folder structures through visual organization.

### 3.2 Data Model for Organization Mode

In Organization Mode, items on the board represent raw files, not IIIF resources:

```json
{
  "@context": [
    "http://www.w3.org/ns/anno.jsonld",
    {
      "fas": "https://example.org/ns/field-archive-studio#",
      "filePath": "fas:filePath",
      "fileHash": "fas:fileHash",
      "extractedMetadata": "fas:extractedMetadata",
      "groupId": "fas:groupId",
      "groupType": "fas:groupType"
    }
  ],
  "id": "https://example.org/boards/org-board/annotations/file-1",
  "type": "Annotation",
  "motivation": "painting",
  "filePath": "/source/IMG_0001.jpg",
  "fileHash": "sha256:abc123...",
  "extractedMetadata": {
    "dateTaken": "2024-06-15T10:30:00Z",
    "gpsLat": 41.8781,
    "gpsLon": -87.6298,
    "cameraModel": "iPhone 15 Pro",
    "orientation": 1
  },
  "groupId": "group-uuid-1",
  "groupType": "manifest",
  "body": {
    "type": "Image",
    "format": "image/jpeg",
    "thumbnail": "data:image/jpeg;base64,..."
  },
  "target": {
    "type": "SpecificResource",
    "source": "https://example.org/boards/org-board/canvas/1",
    "selector": {
      "type": "FragmentSelector",
      "value": "xywh=100,200,150,150"
    }
  }
}
```

### 3.3 Grouping Semantics

Groups in Organization Mode map to Biiif folder conventions:

```json
{
  "id": "group-uuid-1",
  "type": "ManifestGroup",
  "name": "_manuscript_photos",
  "metadata": {
    "label": { "en": ["Medieval Manuscript Photographs"] },
    "summary": { "en": ["High-resolution photographs of MS 123"] }
  },
  "items": ["file-uuid-1", "file-uuid-2", "file-uuid-3"],
  "canvasSets": [
    {
      "basename": "page_001",
      "files": [
        { "id": "file-uuid-1", "role": "primary", "motivation": "painting" },
        { "id": "file-uuid-2", "role": "annotation", "motivation": "supplementing" }
      ]
    }
  ],
  "boundingBox": { "x": 100, "y": 200, "width": 500, "height": 400 },
  "visualStyle": {
    "backgroundColor": "#E8F4E8",
    "borderColor": "#4CAF50",
    "borderStyle": "dashed"
  }
}
```

**Group Types:**

| Type | Biiif Convention | Visual Indicator |
|------|------------------|------------------|
| ManifestGroup | Folder starting with `_` | Green dashed border |
| CollectionGroup | Folder without `_` prefix | Blue solid border |
| CanvasSet | Files sharing basename | Yellow highlight overlay |

### 3.4 Organization Mode UI Components

```

```

### 3.5 Clustering Algorithms

**Temporal Clustering:**
```javascript
// DBSCAN on timestamp data
const temporalCluster = {
  algorithm: "DBSCAN",
  epsilon: 1800000, // 30 minutes in milliseconds
  minPoints: 3,
  distanceMetric: (a, b) => Math.abs(a.dateTaken - b.dateTaken)
};
```

**Spatial Clustering:**
```javascript
// DBSCAN on GPS coordinates
const spatialCluster = {
  algorithm: "DBSCAN",
  epsilon: 50, // meters
  minPoints: 5,
  distanceMetric: haversineDistance
};
```

**Visual Similarity:**
```javascript
// Perceptual hashing for image clustering
const visualCluster = {
  algorithm: "hierarchical",
  hashType: "pHash",
  threshold: 12, // Hamming distance
  linkage: "average"
};
```

### 3.6 Export to Biiif Structure

```
Export Process:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Validate   â”‚ -> â”‚  Transform  â”‚ -> â”‚  Generate   â”‚ -> â”‚   Output    â”‚
â”‚  Groups     â”‚    â”‚  Groups to  â”‚    â”‚  _info.json â”‚    â”‚  Folder     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚    â”‚  Folders    â”‚    â”‚  Files      â”‚    â”‚  Structure  â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Validation Rules:**
- No ManifestGroup nested inside ManifestGroup
- All ManifestGroups contain at least one file
- Canvas sets have a designated primary file
- Folder names are filesystem-safe

---

## 4. Annotation Mode (Post-IIIF)

### 4.1 Purpose

Create semantic connections between IIIF-compliant resources (Manifests, Canvases, regions) using W3C Web Annotations.

### 4.2 Item Sources

Items in Annotation Mode come from IIIF resources:

| Source | Body Type | Display |
|--------|-----------|---------|
| Full Canvas | Canvas IRI | Thumbnail + label |
| Canvas Region | SpecificResource with FragmentSelector | Cropped thumbnail |
| Full Manifest | Manifest IRI | Representative thumbnail + label |
| External Image | Image IRI | Loaded thumbnail |

### 4.3 Annotation Mode UI Components

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

â”‚  â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ â”‚                                                   â”‚  Inspector  â”‚
```

### 4.4 Connection Drawing Workflow

```
1. Select Connection Tool (C key)
     â”‚
     â–¼
2. Click source item or region
     â”‚
     â”œâ”€â”€â”€ If item: whole item selected
     â””â”€â”€â”€ If shift+click: enter region selection mode
                â”‚
                â–¼
         Draw region on item
                â”‚
                â–¼
3. Drag to target item or region
     â”‚
     â–¼
4. Release â†’ Connection Type Selector appears
     â”‚
     â–¼
5. Select type â†’ Optional: add label/notes
     â”‚
     â–¼
6. Web Annotation created and rendered
```

### 4.5 Region-to-Region Connections

For precise scholarly connections, users can link specific regions:

```json
{
  "type": "Annotation",
  "motivation": "linking",
  "body": {
    "type": "TextualBody",
    "value": "Same decorative border motif"
  },
  "target": [
    {
      "type": "SpecificResource",
      "source": "https://example.org/iiif/manifest/123/canvas/1",
      "selector": {
        "type": "SvgSelector",
        "value": "<svg><polygon points='10,10 50,10 50,100 10,100'/></svg>"
      },
      "purpose": "identifying"
    },
    {
      "type": "SpecificResource",
      "source": "https://example.org/iiif/manifest/456/canvas/3",
      "selector": {
        "type": "FragmentSelector",
        "conformsTo": "http://www.w3.org/TR/media-frags/",
        "value": "xywh=200,150,80,120"
      },
      "purpose": "identifying"
    }
  ]
}
```

### 4.6 Confidence/Certainty Extension

Scholarly annotations often require expressing uncertainty:

```json
{
  "@context": [
    "http://www.w3.org/ns/anno.jsonld",
    {
      "certainty": "https://example.org/ns/certainty#",
      "certaintyLevel": "certainty:level",
      "certain": "certainty:certain",
      "probable": "certainty:probable",
      "possible": "certainty:possible",
      "uncertain": "certainty:uncertain",
      "speculative": "certainty:speculative"
    }
  ],
  "type": "Annotation",
  "motivation": "linking",
  "certaintyLevel": "probable",
  "body": {
    "type": "TextualBody",
    "value": "Likely copied from the same exemplar"
  },
  "target": [/* ... */]
}
```

**Visual Indicators for Certainty:**

| Level | Line Style | Opacity | Badge |
|-------|------------|---------|-------|
| Certain | Solid | 100% | âœ“ |
| Probable | Solid | 80% | ? |
| Possible | Dashed | 60% | ?? |
| Uncertain | Dotted | 40% | ??? |
| Speculative | Dotted, light | 25% | ğŸ’­ |

## 5. Canvas Rendering System

### 5.1 Coordinate System

The board canvas uses a coordinate system compatible with IIIF's fragment selector specification:

```
Origin (0,0) â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â–¶ X (width)
    â”‚
    â”‚    Fragment: xywh=x,y,width,height
    â”‚
    â”‚    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
    â”‚    â”‚ (x,y)           â”‚
    â”‚    â”‚    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”‚
    â”‚    â”‚    â”‚ Item  â”‚    â”‚
    â”‚    â”‚    â”‚       â”‚    â”‚
    â”‚    â”‚    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜    â”‚
    â”‚    â”‚     width,heightâ”‚
    â”‚    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
    â”‚
    â–¼
    Y (height)
```

### 5.2 Viewport Management

```javascript
const viewportState = {
  // Current view
  pan: { x: 0, y: 0 },
  zoom: 1.0,
  
  // Constraints
  minZoom: 0.1,
  maxZoom: 10.0,
  
  // Canvas bounds
  canvasWidth: 10000,
  canvasHeight: 10000,
  
  // Viewport in canvas coordinates
  getViewportBounds() {
    const viewWidth = window.innerWidth / this.zoom;
    const viewHeight = window.innerHeight / this.zoom;
    return {
      x: -this.pan.x / this.zoom,
      y: -this.pan.y / this.zoom,
      width: viewWidth,
      height: viewHeight
    };
  }
};
```

### 5.3 Layer System

Layers are implemented as separate AnnotationPages with toggleable visibility:

```json
{
  "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1",
  "type": "Canvas",
  "items": [
    {
      "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1/page/items",
      "type": "AnnotationPage",
      "label": { "en": ["Items"] },
      "items": [/* item annotations */]
    }
  ],
  "annotations": [
    {
      "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1/annotations/connections",
      "type": "AnnotationPage",
      "label": { "en": ["Connections"] },
      "behavior": ["hidden"]
    },
    {
      "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1/annotations/notes",
      "type": "AnnotationPage",
      "label": { "en": ["Notes & Highlights"] }
    },
    {
      "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1/annotations/drawings",
      "type": "AnnotationPage",
      "label": { "en": ["Freehand Drawings"] }
    }
  ]
}
```

**Default Layers:**

| Layer | AnnotationPage | Render Order | Default Visibility |
|-------|----------------|--------------|-------------------|
| Background | (Canvas fill) | 0 | Always |
| Grid | N/A (computed) | 1 | Toggle |
| Items | `/page/items` | 2 | Always |
| Connections | `/annotations/connections` | 3 | Always |
| Highlights | `/annotations/highlights` | 4 | Toggle |
| Notes | `/annotations/notes` | 5 | Always |
| Drawings | `/annotations/drawings` | 6 | Toggle |

### 5.4 Rendering Pipeline

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Load       â”‚ -> â”‚  Filter by  â”‚ -> â”‚  Sort by    â”‚ -> â”‚  Render     â”‚
â”‚  Annotationsâ”‚    â”‚  Viewport   â”‚    â”‚  Layer      â”‚    â”‚  to Canvas  â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
                          â”‚
                          â–¼
                   Spatial Index
                   (R-tree)
```

**Thumbnail Loading Strategy:**

1. Load thumbnails for items in viewport first
2. Preload thumbnails for items within 2x viewport
3. Use placeholder for items outside preload area
4. Progressive loading: low-res â†’ high-res

### 5.5 Connection Rendering

Connections are rendered as SVG paths overlaid on the canvas:

```javascript
const connectionRenderer = {
  renderConnection(conn, sourcePos, targetPos, type) {
    const path = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "path");
    
    // Calculate control points for curved connection
    const midX = (sourcePos.x + targetPos.x) / 2;
    const midY = (sourcePos.y + targetPos.y) / 2;
    const dx = targetPos.x - sourcePos.x;
    const dy = targetPos.y - sourcePos.y;
    
    // Bezier curve path
    const d = `M ${sourcePos.x} ${sourcePos.y} 
               Q ${midX + dy * 0.2} ${midY - dx * 0.2} 
                 ${targetPos.x} ${targetPos.y}`;
    
    path.setAttribute("d", d);
    path.setAttribute("class", `connection connection-${type}`);
    path.setAttribute("marker-end", `url(#arrow-${type})`);
    
    return path;
  }
};
```

**Connection Styles (CSS):**

```css
.connection {
  fill: none;
  stroke-width: 2px;
  pointer-events: stroke;
}

.connection-depicts { stroke: #2196F3; }
.connection-transcribes { stroke: #4CAF50; stroke-dasharray: 5,5; }
.connection-contradicts { stroke: #F44336; stroke-dasharray: 3,3,10,3; }
.connection-precedes { stroke: #9C27B0; }
.connection-relatesTo { stroke: #607D8B; stroke-width: 1px; }

.connection:hover {
  stroke-width: 4px;
  filter: drop-shadow(0 0 4px currentColor);
}

.connection.selected {
  stroke-width: 4px;
  animation: pulse 1s infinite;
}
```

### 6.2 Drag Operations

| Drag Source | Drop Target | Action |
|-------------|-------------|--------|
| Archive item | Canvas (Org) | Add file to board |
| IIIF manifest | Canvas (Ann) | Add manifest item to board |
| Board item | Empty canvas | Move item |
| Board item | Another item | Create connection (if conn tool) |
| Board item | Group boundary | Add to group (Org mode) |
| Lasso selection | N/A | Multi-select items |
| Connection endpoint | Different item | Re-route connection |

### 6.4 Zoom Behavior

```javascript
const zoomConfig = {
  levels: [0.1, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1.0, 1.5, 2.0, 3.0, 5.0, 10.0],
  
  // Zoom to fit all items with padding
  zoomToFit(items, padding = 50) {
    const bounds = this.calculateBounds(items);
    const scaleX = (viewportWidth - padding * 2) / bounds.width;
    const scaleY = (viewportHeight - padding * 2) / bounds.height;
    return Math.min(scaleX, scaleY, this.maxZoom);
  },
  
  // Zoom to specific item
  zoomToItem(item, targetZoom = 1.0) {
    const center = item.getCenter();
    this.animateToPosition(center, targetZoom);
  },
  
  // Semantic zoom levels
  getSemanticZoom(level) {
    if (level < 0.3) return 'overview';      // Show only thumbnails
    if (level < 0.7) return 'summary';       // Show thumbnails + labels
    if (level < 1.5) return 'detail';        // Full detail
    return 'inspect';                         // High detail + metadata
  }
};
```

### 6.5 Click-to-Zoom for Annotations

When an annotation is clicked in a list or search result:

```javascript
function zoomToAnnotation(annotation) {
  const target = annotation.target;
  
  if (target.selector?.type === 'FragmentSelector') {
    const region = parseXYWH(target.selector.value);
    
    // Add padding (20% of region dimensions)
    const padding = {
      x: region.width * 0.2,
      y: region.height * 0.2
    };
    
    const paddedRegion = {
      x: region.x - padding.x,
      y: region.y - padding.y,
      width: region.width + padding.x * 2,
      height: region.height + padding.y * 2
    };
    
    // Animate viewport to region
    viewport.animateToBounds(paddedRegion, {
      duration: 300,
      easing: 'easeOutCubic'
    });
    
    // Highlight the annotation
    annotation.element.classList.add('highlighted');
    setTimeout(() => {
      annotation.element.classList.remove('highlighted');
    }, 2000);
  }
}
```

### 7.1 Organization Mode Tools


**Tool Behaviors:**

| Tool | Click | Drag | Shift+Click |
|------|-------|------|-------------|
| Select | Select item | Move item(s) | Add to selection |
| Lasso | N/A | Draw selection area | Add to selection |
| Group | N/A | Draw group boundary | N/A |
| Canvas Set | Select primary file | N/A | Add to canvas set |

---

## 9. Keyboard Shortcuts

### 9.1 Global Shortcuts

| Shortcut | Action |
|----------|--------|
| `Ctrl/Cmd + S` | Save board |
| `Ctrl/Cmd + Z` | Undo |
| `Ctrl/Cmd + Shift + Z` | Redo |
| `Ctrl/Cmd + A` | Select all items |
| `Ctrl/Cmd + D` | Deselect all |
| `Ctrl/Cmd + F` | Open search |
| `Delete` | Remove selected from board |
| `Escape` | Cancel current operation / deselect |
| `Space` (hold) | Pan mode |
| `+` / `=` | Zoom in |
| `-` | Zoom out |
| `0` | Reset zoom to 100% |
| `1` | Zoom to fit all |
| `Tab` | Cycle through items |

### 9.2 Tool Shortcuts

| Shortcut | Tool |
|----------|------|
| `V` | Select/Move |
| `L` | Lasso select |
| `C` | Connection |
| `R` | Rectangle |
| `P` | Polygon |
| `F` | Freehand |
| `S` | Sticky note |
| `E` | Frame/section |
| `T` | Text label |
| `I` | Region select (on item) |

### 9.3 Organization Mode Shortcuts

| Shortcut | Action |
|----------|--------|
| `G` | Create group from selection |
| `Ctrl/Cmd + G` | Create manifest group |
| `Ctrl/Cmd + Shift + G` | Create collection group |
| `U` | Ungroup |
| `K` | Create canvas set from selection |
| `M` | Toggle manifest/collection type |

### 9.4 Annotation Mode Shortcuts

| Shortcut | Action |
|----------|--------|
| `1-5` | Set connection certainty (1=certain, 5=speculative) |
| `D` | Set connection type: depicts |
| `X` | Set connection type: transcribes |
| `Q` | Set connection type: relates |
| `W` | Set connection type: contradicts |
| `Shift + R` | Reverse connection direction |

### 9.5 Navigation Shortcuts

| Shortcut | Action |
|----------|--------|
| `Arrow keys` | Pan viewport |
| `Shift + Arrow` | Move selected items |
| `Home` | Go to canvas origin |
| `End` | Go to last item |
| `[` | Previous frame/section |
| `]` | Next frame/section |

---

## 10. Export & Persistence

### 10.1 Auto-Save

```javascript
const autoSaveConfig = {
  interval: 30000, // 30 seconds
  debounce: 2000,  // Wait 2s after last change
  
  saveState() {
    return {
      version: "1.0",
      mode: currentMode,
      manifest: boardManifest,
      viewportState: viewport.getState(),
      undoStack: undoManager.getStack(),
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };
  }
};
```

### 10.2 Project File Format

```json
{
  "version": "1.0",
  "id": "project-uuid",
  "name": "Manuscript Analysis Project",
  "mode": "annotation",
  "created": "2025-01-21T10:00:00Z",
  "modified": "2025-01-21T14:30:00Z",
  
  "board": {
    "@context": "http://iiif.io/api/presentation/3/context.json",
    "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid",
    "type": "Manifest"
  },
  
  "annotations": {
    "items": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1/page/items",
    "connections": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1/annotations/connections",
    "notes": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/canvas/1/annotations/notes"
  },
  
  "viewportState": {
    "pan": { "x": 500, "y": 300 },
    "zoom": 0.8
  },
  
  "layerVisibility": {
    "grid": false,
    "connections": true,
    "notes": true,
    "highlights": false
  },
  
  "organizationGroups": [],
  
  "settings": {
    "snapToGrid": true,
    "gridSize": 50,
    "connectionStyle": "curved"
  }
}
```

### 10.3 Export Formats

**Organization Mode Exports:**

| Format | Description | Use Case |
|--------|-------------|----------|
| Biiif Folder | Complete folder structure with files | Direct ingest to iiifBuilder.ts |
| Project JSON | Serialized project state | Backup, collaboration |
| CSV Manifest | Metadata spreadsheet | Batch editing |

**Annotation Mode Exports:**

| Format | Description | Use Case |
|--------|-------------|----------|
| W3C Web Annotation Collection | Full annotation export | Sharing, external systems |
| IIIF Annotation Pages | Per-layer annotation pages | IIIF ecosystem integration |
| Board Manifest | Complete board as IIIF Manifest | Viewing in IIIF viewers |
| PNG/SVG Snapshot | Static image of current view | Documentation, presentations |
| CSV Annotations | Flattened annotation data | Analysis, spreadsheets |

### 10.4 W3C Web Annotation Collection Export

```json
{
  "@context": "http://www.w3.org/ns/anno.jsonld",
  "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/annotations",
  "type": "AnnotationCollection",
  "label": "Manuscript Analysis Board Annotations",
  "total": 25,
  "first": {
    "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/annotations/page/1",
    "type": "AnnotationPage",
    "items": [
      {
        "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/connections/conn-1",
        "type": "Annotation",
        "motivation": "linking"
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

### 10.5 Biiif Export Workflow

```
Organization Board State

         â–¼

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

            â–¼
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
            â”‚
            â–¼
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
            â”‚
            â–¼
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

```

## 11. Performance Considerations

### 11.1 Spatial Indexing

Use R-tree for efficient spatial queries:

```javascript
class BoardSpatialIndex {
  constructor() {
    this.tree = new RBush();
  }
  
  insert(item) {
    const bbox = this.getBoundingBox(item);
    this.tree.insert({
      minX: bbox.x,
      minY: bbox.y,
      maxX: bbox.x + bbox.width,
      maxY: bbox.y + bbox.height,
      item: item
    });
  }
  
  queryViewport(viewport) {
    return this.tree.search({
      minX: viewport.x,
      minY: viewport.y,
      maxX: viewport.x + viewport.width,
      maxY: viewport.y + viewport.height
    }).map(result => result.item);
  }
  
  queryPoint(x, y) {
    return this.tree.search({
      minX: x, minY: y,
      maxX: x, maxY: y
    }).map(result => result.item);
  }
}
```

### 11.2 Virtualized Rendering

Only render items within the viewport plus buffer:

```javascript
const renderConfig = {
  viewportBuffer: 0.5, // 50% extra on each side
  
  getVisibleItems(viewport, allItems) {
    const bufferedViewport = {
      x: viewport.x - viewport.width * this.viewportBuffer,
      y: viewport.y - viewport.height * this.viewportBuffer,
      width: viewport.width * (1 + 2 * this.viewportBuffer),
      height: viewport.height * (1 + 2 * this.viewportBuffer)
    };
    
    return spatialIndex.queryViewport(bufferedViewport);
  }
};
```

### 11.3 Thumbnail Loading Strategy

```javascript
const thumbnailLoader = {
  // Priority queue based on distance from viewport center
  loadQueue: new PriorityQueue((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority),
  
  // Cache loaded thumbnails
  cache: new LRUCache({ max: 500 }),
  
  // Concurrent loading limit
  maxConcurrent: 4,
  
  queueThumbnail(item, viewport) {
    const distance = this.distanceFromCenter(item, viewport);
    const priority = distance < 0 ? 0 : distance; // In viewport = highest priority
    
    this.loadQueue.enqueue({ item, priority });
    this.processQueue();
  },
  
  // Level of detail based on zoom
  getThumbnailSize(zoom) {
    if (zoom < 0.5) return 100;
    if (zoom < 1.0) return 200;
    if (zoom < 2.0) return 400;
    return 800;
  }
};
```

### 11.4 Connection Path Caching

```javascript
const connectionPathCache = {
  cache: new Map(),
  
  getPath(connection) {
    const key = this.getKey(connection);
    
    if (this.cache.has(key)) {
      return this.cache.get(key);
    }
    
    const path = this.calculatePath(connection);
    this.cache.set(key, path);
    return path;
  },
  
  getKey(connection) {
    const source = connection.targets[0];
    const target = connection.targets[1];
    return `${source.position.x},${source.position.y}-${target.position.x},${target.position.y}`;
  },
  
  invalidate(itemId) {
    // Invalidate all connections involving this item
    for (const [key, path] of this.cache.entries()) {
      if (key.includes(itemId)) {
        this.cache.delete(key);
      }
    }
  }
};
```

### 11.5 Debounced Operations

```javascript
const debouncedOperations = {
  // Debounce rapid viewport changes
  updateVisibleItems: debounce((viewport) => {
    const visible = renderConfig.getVisibleItems(viewport, allItems);
    renderer.updateItems(visible);
  }, 16), // ~60fps
  
  // Debounce search
  performSearch: debounce((query) => {
    const results = searchIndex.search(query);
    searchPanel.displayResults(results);
  }, 300),
  
  // Debounce auto-save
  triggerAutoSave: debounce(() => {
    persistence.save(board.getState());
  }, 2000)
};
```

## 12. Accessibility

### 12.1 Keyboard Navigation

```javascript
const keyboardNavigation = {
  // Tab through items in reading order
  getItemOrder() {
    return allItems.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.position.y !== b.position.y) {
        return a.position.y - b.position.y;
      }
      return a.position.x - b.position.x;
    });
  },
  
  // Focus management
  focusItem(item) {
    const element = item.getElement();
    element.setAttribute('tabindex', '0');
    element.focus();
    element.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'true');
    
    // Announce to screen reader
    this.announce(`Selected ${item.label}`);
  },
  
  announce(message) {
    const liveRegion = document.getElementById('aria-live-region');
    liveRegion.textContent = message;
  }
};
```

### 12.2 ARIA Attributes

```html
<!-- Board canvas container -->
<div 
  role="application"
  aria-label="Research board canvas"
  aria-describedby="board-instructions"
>
  <!-- Item element -->
  <div
    role="img"
    aria-label="MS 123 Canvas 1: Folio 1 recto"
    aria-describedby="item-1-desc"
    tabindex="0"
    aria-selected="false"
    aria-grabbed="false"
  >
    <img src="thumbnail.jpg" alt="" />
  </div>
  
  <!-- Connection element -->
  <svg role="img" aria-label="Connection: MS 123 depicts Photo 001">
    <path ... />
  </svg>
  
  <!-- Instructions (hidden visually) -->
  <div id="board-instructions" class="sr-only">
    Use arrow keys to pan. Press Tab to move between items.
    Press C to create a connection from the selected item.
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Live region for announcements -->
<div id="aria-live-region" role="status" aria-live="polite" class="sr-only"></div>
```

### 12.3 High Contrast Mode

```css
@media (prefers-contrast: high) {
  .board-canvas {
    background-color: white;
  }
  
  .board-item {
    border: 3px solid black;
  }
  
  .board-item:focus {
    outline: 4px solid blue;
    outline-offset: 2px;
  }
  
  .connection {
    stroke-width: 4px;
  }
  
  .connection-depicts { stroke: blue; }
  .connection-transcribes { stroke: green; }
  .connection-contradicts { stroke: red; }
}
```

### 12.4 Screen Reader Support

```javascript
const screenReaderSupport = {
  // Describe connections for item
  getConnectionDescription(item) {
    const connections = this.getConnectionsForItem(item);
    
    if (connections.length === 0) {
      return "No connections";
    }
    
    return connections.map(conn => {
      const direction = conn.source === item ? "connects to" : "connected from";
      const target = conn.source === item ? conn.target : conn.source;
      return `${conn.type} ${direction} ${target.label}`;
    }).join(". ");
  },
  
  // Announce item selection
  announceSelection(item) {
    const connDesc = this.getConnectionDescription(item);
    const position = `Position: row ${Math.floor(item.position.y / 100)}, column ${Math.floor(item.position.x / 100)}`;
    
    this.announce(`${item.label}. ${connDesc}. ${position}`);
  }
};
```

### 12.5 Reduced Motion

```css
@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
  .board-canvas,
  .board-item,
  .connection {
    transition: none !important;
    animation: none !important;
  }
  
  /* Use instant viewport changes */
  .viewport-transition {
    transition-duration: 0ms;
  }
}
```

```javascript
const motionPreference = {
  prefersReducedMotion: window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches,
  
  animateViewport(target, duration = 300) {
    if (this.prefersReducedMotion) {
      viewport.jumpTo(target);
    } else {
      viewport.animateTo(target, duration);
    }
  }
};
```

### A.1 Item Placement Annotation

```json
{
  "@context": [
    "http://www.w3.org/ns/anno.jsonld",
    "http://iiif.io/api/presentation/3/context.json"
  ],
  "id": "https://example.org/boards/board-uuid/annotations/item-1",
  "type": "Annotation",
  "motivation": "painting",
  "created": "2025-01-21T12:00:00Z",
  "modified": "2025-01-21T14:30:00Z",
  "creator": {
    "id": "https://example.org/users/researcher-1",
    "type": "Person",
    "name": "Jane Researcher",
    "nickname": "jresearcher"
  },
  "body": {
    "id": "https://example.org/iiif/manifest/123/canvas/1",
    "type": "Canvas",
    "label": { "en": ["Folio 1 recto"] },
    "width": 3000,
    "height": 4000,
    "thumbnail": [{
      "id": "https://example.org/iiif/image/123/full/200,/0/default.jpg",
      "type": "Image",
      "format": "image/jpeg",
      "width": 200,
      "height": 267
    }]
  },
  "target": {
    "type": "SpecificResource",
```

## Appendix C: Integration with iiifBuilder.ts

The Organization Mode output directly feeds into the Biiif pipeline:

### C.1 Export Mapping

| Board Concept | Biiif Output |
|---------------|--------------|
| ManifestGroup | Folder with `_` prefix |
| CollectionGroup | Folder without `_` prefix |
| Canvas Set | Files sharing basename |
| Group Metadata | `_info.json` |
| Canvas Set Metadata | `{basename}_canvas.json` |
| File | Copied/moved to target location |

### C.2 _info.json Generation

From group metadata:

```json
{
  "@context": "https://biiif.org/context.json",
  "type": "ManifestMetadata",
  "label": { "en": ["Medieval Manuscript Photographs"] },
  "summary": { "en": ["High-resolution photographs of MS 123"] },
  "metadata": [
    {
      "label": { "en": ["Date"] },
      "value": { "en": ["June 2024"] }
    }
  ],
  "rights": "http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/4.0/",
  "requiredStatement": {
    "label": { "en": ["Attribution"] },
    "value": { "en": ["Field Survey 2024"] }
  },
  "originalFilenames": {
    "page_001.jpg": "IMG_0001.jpg",
    "page_001_transcript.txt": "notes_page1.txt",
    "page_002.jpg": "IMG_0002.jpg"
  }
}
```

### C.3 Canvas Set JSON Generation

```json
{
  "@context": "https://biiif.org/context.json",
  "type": "CanvasMetadata",
  "id": "page_001",
  "label": { "en": ["Folio 1 recto"] },
  "files": [
    {
      "filename": "page_001.jpg",
      "role": "primary",
      "motivation": "painting",
      "format": "image/jpeg"
    },
    {
      "filename": "page_001_transcript.txt",
      "role": "annotation",
      "motivation": "supplementing",
      "format": "text/plain",
      "language": "en"
    }
  ]
}
```
